\bentry
\word[K(1)]{K, k}
\pron{keV}
\gl{\nA}
\expl{(\bava\ \eng{ks} yA \eng{k's}).}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} iMgilxSf vaNaRmAleya \eng{11}neya akaSxra. 
\num{2} \eng{K} AkArada yAvudeV vasutx. 
\num{3} \eng{K} akaSxrada acucx moLe. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[K(2)]{K}
\pron{?}
\gl{\saMkiSx}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (\beY) \eng{King(s)}. 
\num{2} \eng{Kochel} (moVsAZTaRna saMgiVta kaqtigaLa kAyxTalAgu). 
\num{3} \eng{Kelvin(s)}. 
\numi{4} (\eng{k} saha) (aMkiya taruvAya) 
\banum
\alnum{a} (kaMpUyxTarf) \eng{1024} (aMdare \eng{$2^\bg 10\eg$}) beYTugaLu athavA saDilavAgi \eng{1000} beYTugaLu. 
\alnum{b} \eng{1000}. 
\eanum
\numie
\enum
\emng

\pron{kejari(V)}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng

\banum

\alnum{b} miVnu, akikx, moTeTx \mo vanunx hAki mADida yUroVpinavara oMdu aDige padAthaR. 
\eanum
\emng

\bentry

\pron{kiVlf}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (haDagina) aDimara; pATaNa; benunx tole; taLa tole; haDagina yA doVNiya meYgelalx AdhAravAgi taLadalilx udadxkUkx hAkiruva marada aDigaTuTx,dimimx. 
\num{2} (haDagugaLa loVhada) aDigaTuTx; aDi halagegaLu. 
\num{3} (\kaparx) haDagu. 
\num{4} (\pArxvi) edeyeVNu; halavu pakiSxjAtigaLa ede mULegaLa udadxkUkx iruva ububx, ENu. 
\num{5} (\savi) ENudaLa(gaLu); hUvina daLavalaya \mo vugaLalilxruva, haDagina aDi toleyanunx hoVluva, joVDi daLa. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng

\emng

\bentry
\word[keep(1)]{keep}
\pron{kiVpf}
\gl{\kirx}
\expl{(\BU\ matutx \BUkaq\ \eng{kept} \ucAcx\ kepfTx).}


\noindent
\gl{\sakirx}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (kAyide, vAgAdxna, tananxlilxTaTx naMbike, kwlu, karAru, nishicxta BeVTi, \mo vanunx) pAlisu; anusarisu; naDesu; gwravisu: \eng{keep one's word} mAtina parxkAra naDe. 
\num{2} (hababx, varxta, \mo vanunx) mADu; naDesu; neraveVrisu; Acarisu. 
\num{3} (vayxkitx, dugaR, paTaTxNa, phuTfbAlina goVlu, \mo vanunx) kAyu; kApADu; rakiSxsu; \eng{God keep you} deVvaru ninanxnunx rakiSxsali. 
\num{4} noVDiko; (oMdara) javAbAdxrivahisu: \eng{keep children} makakxLanunx noVDiko. 
\num{5} (vashadalilxruva vasutxvanunx) irisiko; iTuTxko: \eng{you may keep the change} cilalxreyanunx (vApAsu mADabeVkAgilalxde) niVneV iTuTxko. 
\num{6} (mane \mo vanunx) cenAnxgi, cokakxTavAgi, sariyAda sithxtiyalilx -- iTuTxko. 
\num{7} (aMgaDi \mo vanunx) sariyAgi nivaRhisu, iTuTxko; naDesikoMDu hoVgu. 
\num{8} (dinacari, lekAkxcArada pusatxka, \mo vanunx vivaragaLanenxlalx dAKalu mADi) karxmavAgi irisu, iDu, iTiTxru. 
\num{9} (kuTuMba, tAnu, \mo vanunx) salahu; hore; noVDiko; poVSisu; jiVvanoVpAya odagisi iTuTxko, iTuTxkoMDiru. 
\num{10} (hasugaLu, jeVnuhuLu, \mo vanunx) sAku; sAki iTuTxko: \eng{keep bees} jeVnu sAku. 
\num{11} (obAbxkeyanunx upaBoVgakAkxgi. upapatinxyanAnxgi, raKAvf Agi) iTuTxkoMDiru; maDagikoMDiru. 
\num{12} (sarakanunx, mAlanunx) mArATakekx sadA -- hoMdiru. iTiTxru: \eng{do you keep buttons} niVvu guMDigaLanunx (mArATakekx) iTiTxdidxVrA? 
\num{13} uLisiTuTxkoMDiru; kApADiTuTxkoMDiru; asitxtavxdalilxTuTxkoMDiru. 
\num{14} (vayxkitxyanunx sereyalilx, baMdhanadalilx) iTiTxru; hiDidiTiTxru. 
\num{15} takakx yA sUcita sithxtiyalilx iTuTxkoMDiru: \eng{keep them happy} avaranunx saMtoVSavAgiTuTxkoMDiru. 
\num{16} (vayxkitxyanunx, tananxnenxV, yAvudeV kelasavanunx mADadaMte) taDe; niroVdhisu; taDehiDi: \eng{will keep you from going too fast} atiyAda veVgadalilx hoVgadaMte ninanxnunx taDeyutAtxne. 
\num{17} (vayxkitxyanunx seremaneyalilx \mo\ kaDe) hiDidiDu; taDedu nililxsu: \eng{what kept you so long?} ninanxnunx iSuTx hotutx yAvudu taDeditutx, hiDidiTiTxtutx? 
\num{18} (yAvudeV vasutxvanunx, muMdina upayoVgakAkxgi) uLisiTiTxru; baLasade iTiTxru; kAdirisu; kAdiDu: \eng{keep it for tomorrow} nALege uLisiTiTxru. 
\hypertarget{keep(19)}{} 
\num{19} mucicxTiTxru; bacicxTiTxru; goVpayxvAgi, guTATxgi, rahasayxvAgi -- iTiTxru: \eng{keep one's} \hyperref{kandict_c.pdf}{C}{counsel(1) nuga(2)}{$^1$counsel}. tananx iMgitavanunx goVpayxvAgiDu; aBipArxyavanunx biTuTx koDadiru; bAyi biDadiru; mwnavAgiru. 
\num{20} (dAri, mADutitxruva kelasa, \mo vanunx) anusarisutAtx hoVgu; biDade mADutAtx hoVgu; hiDidiru; biDadiru: \eng{he keeps his own course} avanu tananx dAriyanenxV hiDiyutAtxne. 
\num{21} (hAsige, koThaDi, mane, \mo vanunx) biTuTx baradiru; (hAsige \mo vugaLalelxV) iru. 
\num{22} (parxtiBaTaneyanunx lekikxsade, kudureya meVle, keSxVtarx, raMgasathxLa, niMta nele, itAyxdiyalilx) kadaladiru; BadarxvAgiru; tananx sAthxna biDadiru, badalAyisadiru. 
\num{23} (oMdu niyatavAda sathxLadalilx, jAgadalilx) iDu; irisu: \eng{knives are kept in this drawer} I seLeKAneyalilx cAkugaLanunx iTiTxde. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\akirx}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (maneyoLageV) iru: \eng{keep indoors} maneyoLageV iru. 
\num{2} (\AmA, \kanmu\ keVMbirxjf \vivi) iru; vAsisu: \eng{where do you keep?} niVnu elilx ididxVye? elilx vAsavAgididxVye? 
\num{3} (yAvudeV hesarisida sithxtiyalilx) iru: \eng{keep in good health} AroVgayxvaMtanAgiru. \eng{keep cool} shAMtanAgiru. 
\num{4} (nideRVshisida, hesarisida, dikukx, dAri, kAyaR, \mo vugaLalilx) sAgiru; muMduvariyutitxru: \eng{keep straight on for two miles} inUnx eraDu meYli neVravAgi muMduvariyutitxru. \eng{she keeps giggling} Ake kisakisane nagutatxleV irutAtxLe. 
\num{5} (AhAra padAthaR, \mo vugaLa \vi) hadageDadiru; haLasadiru; keDadiru. 
\num{6} (\rUpa\ sudidx, \mo vugaLa \vi) haLasi hoVgadiru; muMdina saMdaBaRdalilx baLasuvaMtiru. 
\num{7} (kirxkeTfnalilx) vikeTuTxgaLanunx -- kAyu, rakiSxsu.

\bentry
\word[key(1)]{key}
\pron{kiV}
\gl{\nA}
\expl{(\bava\ \eng{keys}).}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} kiV; kiVlikeY; biVgada -- keY, esaLu. 
\num{2} kiVlikeY; biVgada keY; bayasidadxnunx paDeyalu, udidxSaTx kAyaRvanunx sAdhisalu neravAguva yA aDiDxpaDisuva vasutx, sAdhana, \mo vu. 
\hypertarget{key(1)3}{} 
\num{3} (\bava dalilx) saMta piVTarana utatxrAdhikAriyAgi poVpanige vahisikoDuva caciRna adhikAra. 
\num{4} kiVli keY; biVgada keY; tananx saninxveVshada baladiMda samudarx, BUBAga, \mo vugaLa meVle hatoVTi koDuva AyakaTiTxna nele, sAthxna: \eng{Gibraltor is the key of the Mediterranean} jibArxlaTxrf koVTeyu meDiTareVniyanf samudarxkekx kiVlikeY yA parxveVshadAvxra Agide. 
\num{5} (ajAcnxta, rahasayx yA asapxSaTx Agiruvudanunx parxkaTagoLisuva, tiLisuva yA vivarisuva) kiVlikeY; vivaraNe yA utatxra. 
\num{6} (anayxBASiVya pusatxkada) akaSxrAnuvAda; shAbidxka BASAMtara; padakekx padaviTaTx anuvAda. 
\hypertarget{key(1)7}{} 
\num{7} (caduraMgadATada samaseyxyanunx biDisuvalilxna) modala naDe; parxthama calane. 
\num{8} kiVlikeY (pusatxka); gaNita samaseyxgaLu \mo vugaLanunx biDisuva vidhAnagaLanunx tiLisi, mAdari nidashaRnagaLanunx koDuva pusatxka. 
\num{9} kiVlikeY; BeVdana saMkeVta; gUDhalipi yA rahasayx barahagaLanunx Odalu sahAyakavAda pada yA vayxvasethx. 
\num{10} (\saM) parxdhAna savxraparxsAtxra; oMdu nidiRSaTx savxravanunx avalaMbisi, parasapxra sapxSaTxvAgi saMbaMdha hoMdidudx, kaqtiyalilx parxdhAnavAgiruva, savxra -- samucacxya, vayxvasethx, parxsAtxra, padadhxti, taMDa. 
\num{11} (\rUpa) (aBipArxyada yA aBivayxkitxya, vicArada yA mAtina) riVti; sheYli; dhoVraNe. 
\num{12} kUDukiVlu; kUDubeNe; beVre beVre tuMDugaLanunx kUDisi bigigoLisalu saMdugaLalilx nATuva, marada yA loVhada beNe, gUTa. 
\num{13} (dabebxgaLa naDuve metitx, avugaLanunx kUDisi, BadarxgoLisalu taDike goVDege metutxva) gAreya -- modala baLita, modala leVpa, modala metutxve. 
\num{14} (gAre \mo vu metitxkoLaLxlu sahAyakavAda) oraTu meVlemxY. 
\num{15} (AgaRnf, piyAnoV, \mo\ vAdayxgaLalilx nAda horaDisalu, beraLacucx yaMtarxdalilx beraLacucx mADalu, tUtu mADalu, \mo vugaLigAgi beraLiniMda otutxva) guMDi; kiVlu; biraDe. 
\num{16} viduyxtf guMDi, kiVlu, \udA\ TeligArxphfZ yA beMki hotitxsuva yaMtarxgaLalilx viduyxnamxMDalavanunx pUNaRgoLisalu yA kaDidu hAkalu baLasuva yAMtirxka sAdhna. 
\num{17} tirupu keY; kiVlikeY; \kanmu\ gaDiyAra \mo vugaLa tirupumoLe, tirupu bilelx, \mo vugaLanunx hiDidu tirugisuva sAdhana. 
\num{18} (sikamoVrf, AyxSf, \mo\ maragaLa) rekekxkAyi; rekekxbiVja; pakakxgaLalilx rekekxgaLaMtha eraDu teLu elegaLu aMTikoMDiruva kAyi yA biVja. 
\num{19} (aneVka veVLe \bava dalilx) otutxguMDi; beraLacucx yaMtarx, kaMpUyxTarf, \mo vugaLanunx cAlanegoLisalu baLasuva otutxguMDigaLalilx oMdu.

\num{1} mUtarxpiMDa; kalija; kasheVrukagaLa hoTeTxyoLage benenxlubina baLi iruva, neYTorxVjanfyuta nirupayukatx padAthaRgaLanunx deVhadiMda visajiRsuvudakAkxgi mUtarxvanunx utapxtitx mADuva garxMthijoVDi. \imglink{kidneyfigure}{\raisebox{-0.15cm}[0pt][0pt] {\pdfimage width 0.5cm height 0.5cm {K_Pictures/kidney.jpg}}} 
\num{2} (AhAravAgi baLasuva kuri, dana, haMdi, \mo vugaLa) mUtarxpiMDa. 
\num{3} parxkaqti; savxBAva: \eng{a man of that kidney} aMtha parxkaqtiya manuSayx. \eng{a man of the right kidney} oLeLxya savxBAvadavanu. 
\hypertarget{kidney(4)}{} 
\num{4} aMDAkArada AlUgeDeDx. 
\enum
\emng

\bentry

\pron{kilf}
\gl{\sakirx}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} kolulx; koMdu hAku; sAyisu; pArxNa tege; sAvige, maraNakekx guri mADu. 
\num{2} (roVga, duHKa, AGAta, madayxpAna, viSapAna, \mo vugaLa \vi) sAyisu; sAvanunxMTumADu; sAvanunx taru; sAvige kAraNavAgu. 
\num{3} (kathe \mo vugaLalilx, pAtarxvanunx) kolulx; sAyisu; satatxMte nirUpisu: \eng{kill your villain in the last chapter} ninanx KaLanAyakananunx koneya adhAyxyadalilx kolulx. 
\num{4} (giDa, roVga, \mo vugaLa) satatxvXnAsha mADu; jiVva tege. 
\num{5} (BAvagaLu \mo vanunx) konegANisibiDu; aDagisi biDu; aLiyisu; dhavxMsa mADu. 
\num{6} (baNaNx \mo vanunx, vayxtirikatxvAda baNaNx \mo vugaLiMda) kaLeguMdisu; nisetxVjagoLisu; vivaNaRgoLisu; niSapxrXBAvagoLisu. 
\num{7} (BaviSayxtatxnunx edurunoVDutAtx, BAviV GaTaneyanunx niriVkiSxsutAtx) hotutx kaLe; kAla taLuLx; (vayxthaRvAgi) samaya poVlu mADu. 
\num{8} (BAri mecicxge, KuSi, vinoVda, \mo vugaLalilx obabxnanunx) muLugisi biDu; paravashagoLisu: \eng{dressed to kill} paravashagoLisuvaMte beDaginiMda yA AkaSaRkavAgi siMgarisikoMDa, alaMkarisikoMDa. 
\num{9} (lAnf Tenisf) (hiMdakekx kaLuhalAgadaMte, ceMDanunx) bArisu; hoDe. 
\num{10} (phuTfbAlf) (muMdakekx calisadaMte ceMDanunx) taDedu biDu; nililxsibiDu; nishacxlagoLisu. 
\num{11} (pAliRmeMTinalilx, masUdeyanunx) hata mADibiDu; koMdu hAku; nipAta mADibiDu; pUtiRyAgi soVlisibiDu; tale etatxdaMte mADibiDu; huTaTxDagisibiDu. 
\num{12} (husi dayeyiMda, dayA BArxMtiyiMda) keDakuMTumADu; hAniyuMTumADu. 
\num{13} pArxNigaLanunx koMdu mAMsa paDe. 
\num{14} (\AmA) tiVvarx yAtane koDu; bahaLa noVvuMTumADu: \eng{my feet are killing me} nananx kAlaDigaLu nananxnunx kolulxtitxve, nanage sahisalArada noVvu koDutitxve. 
\num{15} (\AmA) (tiMDi tiVthaRgaLa \vi) dhavxMsa mADibiDu; (tiMdu, kuDidu) KAli mADibiDu. 
\num{16} (honalu beLaku, yaMtarx, \mo vanunx) Arisu; nililxsu. 
\numi{17} (\AtAmx) 
\banum
\alnum{a} joVrAgi, gaTiTxyAgi -- nagu. 
\alnum{b} mitimiVri sharxmisi, vipariVta kelasa mADi baLalu: \eng{don't kill yourself lifting them all at once} oMdeV bArige avelalxvanUnx oTiTxge etitx susAtxgabeVDa, baLalabeVDa. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{18} (\AmA) kaMpUyxTarf pheYlfniMda(oMdu sAlu, pAyxrA, \mo vanunx) -- tegeduhAku, kitutxhAku.

\noindent
\gl{\akirx}
\bmng
\bnum

\num{2} kolulxva haMtakekx, hadakekx baMdiru: \eng{pigs do not kill well at that age} A vayasisxnalilx haMdigaLu kolulxva hadakekx baMdiruvudilalx. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} \eng{kill off} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (bahaLa jana \mo varanunx) koMdubiDu; mugisibiDu; koMdu hAku. 
\alnum{b} (bahaLa vasutxgaLu \mo vanunx) pUtiR nAshamADu, dhavxMsamADu. 
\alnum{c} (garxMthakataRna \vi) (pAtarxvanunx) sAyisu; sAyuvaMte nirUpisu.

\numie
\num{2} \eng{kill oneself} (\AmA) anagatayxvAgi sharxmapaDu; anAvashayxkavAgi sharxmisu; mitimiVri duDi. 
\num{3} \eng{kill or cure} (auSadhagaLa \vi\ yA rUpa) uLisu yA aLisu; badukisu yA sAyisu; (roVgiyanunx) guNapaDisu yA kolulx. 
\num{4} \eng{kill with kindness} ati pirxVtiyiMda yA mudidxniMda (obabxnige)--hAni mADu, hALu mADu, keDaku taru. 
\num{5} \eng{shoot to kill} (keVvala ecacxrike koDalu, bedarisalu yA gAyagoLisalu Agirade) kolalxleMdeV, sAyisuvudakAkxgiyeV -- guMDu hArisu.

\bentry
\word[kind(1)]{kind}
\pron{keYMDf}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (sasayx, pArxNi, \mo vugaLa) buDakaTuTx; kula: \eng{human kind} mAnava kula. 
\num{2} jAti; sAvxBAvika vagaR; \eng{rabbit kind} molada jAti. 
\num{3} (\kerxY) parxBuBoVjana saMsAkxradalilx viniyoVgisuva berxDuDx yA veYnu. 
\num{4} (heVLutitxruva viSaya kaTuTxniTATxdadadxlalx, niSakxqqSaTxvAdadadxlalx, yA utepxrXVkeSxya mAtu, eMdu muMtAgi sUcisuvalilx) EnoV oMdu bageya; oMdu -- namUneya, vidhada, terana, tarahada: \eng{he is a kind of millionaire} avanu oMdu bageya lakASxdhipati. \eng{I felt a kind of compunction} nanage EnoV oMdu bageya anutApa yA pashAcxtAtxpa uMTAyitu. 
\num{5} (\pArxparx) nisagaR, parxkaqti; nisagaRda -- karxma vayxvasethx. 
\num{6} (vayxkitx \mo vakekx) sahajavAda -- mAgaR, riVti, savxBAva, vidhAna: \eng{they act after their kind} tamamx tamamx sahaja riVtige takakxMte avaru vatiRsutAtxre. 
\num{7} savxBAva; parxkaqti; guNa; lakaSxNa: \eng{they differ in kind not merely in degree} avugaLigiruva vayxtAyxsa parxmANaBeVdavaSeTxV alalx, guNaBeVda kUDa. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{law of kind} nisagaRda niyama. 
\num{2} \eng{kind of} (\AmA) savxlapxmaTiTxge: \eng{I had kind of expected it} nAnu savxlapxmaTiTxge adanunx niriVkiSxsidedx. 
\hyperdef{K}{kind(1) pagu(3)}{} 
\numi{3} \eng{nothing of the kind} 
\banum
\alnum{a} A teranadalalxveV alalx. aMthadalalxveV alalx; hAgalalxveV alalx. 
\alnum{b} (nirAkaraNe sUcisuvalilx) KaMDita ilalx; bilfkulf ilalx; sutarAM ilalx. 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{4} \eng{of a kind} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (tirasAkxradalilx) yAvudoV oMdu bageya: \eng{we had coffee of a kind} namage yAvudoV oMdu bageya kAphi sikikxtu; EnoV hesarige kAphi enunxvudu sikikxtu. 
\alnum{b} oMdu muKayxvAda aMshadalilx, riVtiyalilx -- oMdeV riVtiya, oMdeV terana, oMdeV bageya: \eng{they're two of a kind} avaribabxrU (oMdu muKayxvAda aMshadalilx) oMdeV bageyavaru. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{5} \eng{of its kind} adeV vagaRda; adeV vagaRkekx seVrida; adara bageya parimitiyalilx; adaraMtha: \eng{good of its kind} adaraMthadadxralilx oLeLxyadu. 
\num{6} \eng{one's own kind} tananxMthavaru; tananx samAnaru; tanonxDane aneVka samAnAMshagaLanunx hoMdiruvavaru; tananx sadaqsharu. 
\num{7} \eng{something of the kind} parxsakatx vasutxvina yA viSayada bageyadu yAvudoV oMdu; aMthadedxV oMdu; adeV tarahada oMdu. 
\num{8} \eng{the kind of} bageya; terana; taraheya; vidhada: \eng{this is the kind of thing I meant} nananx manasisxnalilxdudxdu I bageya viSaya; nAnu heVLabayasidudx I vidhada viSaya. 
\num{9} \eng{this (}\engit{or} \eng{these) kind of} (\AmA) I bageya: \eng{this kind of men annoy me} I bageya jana nanage kirikiri uMTu mADutAtxre, siTuTx barisutAtxre. 
\num{10} \eng{what kind of} eMtaha; eMtha; yAva bageya, riVtiya, jAtiya: \eng{what kind of tree is this?} idu yAva jAtiya mara? 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\nuga}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{a kind of} (baLasiruva padadalilx oMdu riVtiya, bageya asapxSaTxte, utepxrXVkeSx, \mo vugaLanunx sUcisuvalilx): \eng{a kind of Kumaravyasa of our times} namamx kAlada oMdu riVtiya kumAravAyxsanaMte.

\alnum{b} (\rUpa) aMteyeV; adeV riVtiyalilx; adeV rUpadalilx: \eng{repay his insolence in kind} avana sokikxge badalu sokakxnenxV toVru.

\pron{niV}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (manuSayxna, pArxNiya) maMDi; moNakAlu; jAnu. 
\num{2} (kuLitiruva vayxkitxya) toDe; toDeya meVlABxga: \eng{hold the child on one's knee} maguvanunx toDeya meVle kUrisiko. 
\num{3} maMDiya, moNakAla -- sutitxna jAga. 
\num{4} maMDi; uDupinalilx maMDiyanunx mucucxva BAga. 
\num{5} maMDi; AkAradalilx yA sAthxnadalilx maMDiyanunx hoVluva yAvudeV vasutx, \kanmu\ oMdu koVnadalilx bagigxsida marada yA kabibxNada tuMDu, `gArxphf'nalilx kaDidAda tiruvu \mo vu.

\emng

\noindent
\gl{\nuga}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{bend (}\engit{or} \eng{bow) the knee} (\kanmu\ sharaNAgatiyalilx) maMDiyUru; maMDi bAgisu. 
\num{2} \eng{be on the knees of the Gods} deVvara keYyalilxru; deYvAyatatxvAgiru; Pala anishicxtavAgiru. 
\num{3} \eng{bring (person) to his or her knees} (vayxkitxyanunx) kAligeragisu; sharaNAgatananAnxgi mADu; kAlige biVLisu; kAlige biVLuva sithxtige taru. 
\numi{4} \eng{give a knee to} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (kusitxyalilx yA muSiTxkALagadalilx) jaTiTxyanunx (sULugaLa naDuve) tananx maMDiya meVletitxkoMDu sudhArisikoLuLxvaMte mADu. 
\alnum{b} (kusitx \mo vugaLalilx obabxna) beMbaliganAgu; samathaRkanAgu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{5} \eng{on bended knee(s), on one's knee(s)} (beVDikoLuLxvalilx yA pArxthaRneyalilx, yA sharaNAgatanAdAga) maMDiyUri(koMDu). 
\enum
\emng

\pron{nelf}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} sAvina gaMTe; maraNa GaMTAnAda; obabxna maraNakAladalilx yA shavasaMsAkxradalilx, nidhAnavAgiyU gaMBiVravAgiyU bArisuva GaMTA -- nAda, rava. 
\num{2} (\rUpa) apashakuna; aMtayxda GoVSaNe; avasAnada parxkaTane; apAyada sUcane; maraNada yA vinAshada sUcane, shakuna eMdu parigaNitavAda GoVSaNe, GaTane, \mo vu. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[knell(2)]{knell}
\pron{nelf}
\gl{\sakirx}
\bmng
(maraNa GaMTAnAda mADuvaMte) sAru; GoVSisu. 
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\akirx}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (GaMTeya \vi\ maraNakAladalilx yA shavasaMsAkxradalilx) bArisu; maraNa GaMTAnAda mADu. 
\num{2} goVLudanigare; roVdana dhavxnimADu. 
\num{3} (\rUpa) ashuBasUcakavAda, amaMgaLakaravAda -- savxra etutx, danitege. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\nuga}
\bmng
\eng{ring the knell of} maraNagaMTe bArisu; yAvudeV oMdara aMtayxvanunx yA vinAshavanunx GoVSisu, sAru. 
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word{knickerbocker}
\pron{nikarfbAkarf}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} (\eng{Knickerbocker}) 
\banum
\alnum{a} nUyxyAkiRnavanu. 
\alnum{b} nUyxyAkiRnalilx moTaTx modalu baMdu nelesida Dacacxra saMtatiyava. 
\hypertarget{knickerbocker(2)}{} 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} (\bava dalilx) nikarfbAkarfsx; maMDicalalxNa; moNakAlu caDiDx; moNakAlina baLi niri kaTiTxda, saDilavAda calalxNa. \imglink{knicker bockersfigure}{\raisebox{-0.15cm}[0pt][0pt]{\pdfimage width 0.5cm height 0.7cm {K_Pictures/knicker bockers.jpg}}} 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng

\emng

\bentry
\word[knife(1)]{knife}
\pron{neYphf}
\gl{\nA}
\expl{(\bava\ \eng{knives} \ucAcx\ neYvfsx). }
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (vasutxgaLanunx katatxrisuva sAdhanavAgi yA AyudhavAgi baLasuva) cUri; cAku; katitx: \eng{carving knife} (mAMsa \mo vanunx) hecucxva, katatxrisuva -- cUri. \eng{clasp knife} maDicu cAku, cUri; alaganunx maDisi hiDikeyalilx tUrisiDabahudAda cAku. \eng{pocket knife} jeVbina cAku; jeVbinalilxTuTxkoLaLxbahudAda cikakx cAku. 
\num{2} (yaMtarxda) alagu; katatxrisuva BAga. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent\gl{\nuga}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{at knife-point} cAkuguriyAgi; cAkuedurinalilx; cAkuvina tivitada apAyakekx, bedarikege oLagAgi. 
\num{2} \eng{before you can say knife} (\AmA) `A' enunxvaSaTxralilx; `cAku' enunxvaSaTxralilx; haThAtAtxgi; kaSxNakAladalilx. 
\numi{3} \eng{get one's knife into (a person)} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (obabxna meVle) katitx mase; devxVSakAru; hagesAdhisu; badadhxveYra tALu. 
\alnum{b} (obabxnanunx) dayadAkiSxNayxvilalxde citarxhiMsemADu; marukavilalxde kADu; nidaRyavAgi piVDisu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{4} \eng{have a horror of the knife} shasatxrXcikitesxyeMdare digilu -- biVLu, vipariVta bedaru. 
\hyperdef{K}{knife(1) nuga(5)}{} 
\num{5} \eng{play a good knife and fork} manadaNiye UTa mADu; kaMThapUtiR tinunx; hoTeTx biriya tinunx. 
\numi{6} \eng{that one could cut with a knife} (\AmA) (ucAcxraNe, vAtAvaraNa, \mo vugaLa \vi) 
\banum
\alnum{a} susapxSaTxvAda; suvishadavAda. 
\alnum{b} usirukaTiTxsuva; mukAtxvakAshavilalxda; mukatxvalalxda. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{7} \eng{the knife} shasatxrXcikitesx. 
\numi{8} \eng{war to the knife} 
\banum
\alnum{a} nidaRya samara; kaThoVra kadana; leVshamAtarxvU daye dAkiSxNayxvilalxde naDesuva yudadhx. 
\alnum{b} badadhxdevxVSa; kaDuhage(tana). 
\eanum
\numie
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[knight(1)]{knight}
\pron{neYTf}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} neYTf: 
\banum
\alnum{a} (ULigamAnayx yugadalilx rAjana yA phUyxDalf nAyakana) seYnika anuyAyi; seVnAnucara. 
\alnum{b} (\ca) (madhayx yugada Sivalirx vayxvasethxyalilx yudadhxdalolxV kASxtarxkalegaLa paMdayxdalolxV tananx olavu gwravagaLige pAtarxLAda variSaThx mahiLeya rakaSxNa dhuriVNanU anucaranU Agi tananx pwruSa parAkarxmagaLanunx toVrisutitxdadx) viVrayoVdha; gaMDugali(\rUpa\ saha). 
\alnum{c} (unanxta kulajanAgi peVjf matutx sekxvXVrf dajeRgaLa kASxtarxkalegaLa paMdayxgaLalilx parAkarxma hAgU kASxtarxkalA pArxviVNayxvanunx toVrisi rAjaniMdaloV beVrAva ahaR vayxkitxyiMdaloV saMBAvitanAgi) neYTf padavige ErisalapxTaTxvanu. 
\alnum{d} (veYyakitxka yoVgayxtege yA rAjanigoV deVshakokxV salilxsida seVvege purasAkxravAgi) neYTf padavi paDedavanu. 
\hypertarget{knight(1)1e}{} 
\alnum{e} (\ca) (birxTiSf pAliRmeMTinalilx) yAvudeV SeYrf yA jilelxya parxtinidhi. 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{2} (pArxciVna \roVca) 
\banum
\alnum{a} rAvuta; ashAvxroVhi seYnika. 
\alnum{b} (modalige) roVmanf seVneya rAvuta paDe. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{3} (pArxciVna \girxVca) athenfsx rAjayxda divxtiVya sherxVNiya parxje. 
\num{4} (caduraMga) kudure; kudure taleya kAyi. \imglink{knightfigure}{\raisebox{-0.25cm}[0pt][0pt]{\pdfimage width 0.5cm height 0.6cm {K_Pictures/knight.jpg}}} 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{knight} \hyperref{kandict_b.pdf}{B}{bachelor pagu}{bachelor} (yAvudeV oMdu visheVSa vagaRkekx seVrada) sAmAnayx neYTf. 
\num{2} \eng{knight commander} (unanxta dajeRya neYTfhuDf vagaRgaLalilx yAvudakekxV sadasayxnAda) neYTf kamAMDaru. 
\num{3} \eng{Knight hospitaller} (\bava\ \eng{Knights Hospitaller}) sumAru \kirxsha\ \eng{$1050$}ralilx sAthxpitavAda yoVdhasaMnAyxsigaLa oMdu saMsethx. 
\num{4} \eng{knight} \hyperref{kandict_m.pdf}{M}{marshal(1) pagu(2)}{$^1$marshal} (nAyxya niNARyaka kataRvayxgaLuLaLx) rAja parivArada adhikAri. 
\num{5} \eng{knight of the post} suLuLx sAkaSxyXviVra; suLuLxsAkaSxyX parxviVNa; suLuLx sAkaSxyX niVDi hoTeTx horeyuvavanu. 
\numi{6} \eng{knight of the road} 
\banum
\alnum{a} dArigaLaLx; hAdigaLaLx; hAdikAyudx sulige mADuvavanu. 
\alnum{b} peVri vAyxpAri; saMcAri vAyxpAri; tirugu vAyxpAri. 
\alnum{c} alemAri; aDADxLi; kelasa ilalxde UriMda Urige aleyuvavanu. 
\alnum{d} lAri yA TAyxkisx cAlaka. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{7} \eng{knight of the shire} = \hyperlink{knight(1)1e}{$^1$knight(1, e)}. 
\num{8} \eng{Knight} \hyperref{kandict_t.pdf}{T}{templar pagu}{templar} (\bava\ \eng{Knights Templars}.) 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\pron{nAbf}
\gl{\kirx}
\expl{(\BU\ matutx \BUkaq\ \eng{knobbed}, \vakaq\ \eng{knobbing}).}


\noindent
\gl{\sakirx}
\bmng
gubuTodagisu; gubuTugaLanunx -- iDu, joVDisu, seVrisu. 
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\akirx}
\bmng
gubaTAgu; gubaTu gubaTAgu; uMDuMDeyAgi ubibxko. 
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word{knobble}
\pron{nAbf(ba)lf}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
puTaTx gubaTu; kirugubaTu. 
\emng
\eentry

\emng

\bentry
\word[knock(1)]{knock}
\pron{nAkf}
\gl{\sakirx}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (sadAdxguvaMte balavAgi) hoDe; baDi; kuTuTx; gududx: \eng{he knocked the table thrice} avanu meVjanunx mUru bAri kuTiTxda. 
\num{2} (yAvudanenxV) hoDedu (adaralilx tUtu \mo vanunx) mADu: \eng{knock a hole in the wall} hoDedu goVDeyalilx tUtu mADu. 
\num{3} (\ashi) KaMDisu; kaTuvAgi TiVkisu; vAkapxrXhAra mADu. 
\num{4} (\birx) (\ashi) manasisxna meVle balavAgi -- acocxtutx, muderxyotutx, parxBAva biVru; beraguMTumADu; cakitagoLisu: \eng{what knocks me is his impudence} nananxnunx beragugoLisuvudeMdare avana dhASaTxyXR. 
\num{5} (\birx) (\ashi) peTuTx; saMBoVgisu; jaDi; gumumx. 
\numi{6} baDidu, hoDedu (vasutx, vayxkitxyanunx) 
\banum
\alnum{a} oLakekx taLuLx, hogisu, dUDu, dabubx: \eng{knocked the ball into the hole} ceMDanunx kuLiyoLakekx hoDede, kuLiyoLakekx taLiLxde. 
\alnum{b} horakekx, Acege, modalAgi ODisu, aTuTx, dUDu, taLuLx: \eng{knocked those ideas out of his head} A BAvanegaLanunx nAnu avana taleyiMda, manasisxniMda Acege dUDide, ODiside, aTiTxde. 
\eanum
\numie
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\akirx}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (oLakekx parxveVshisalu) bAgilu taTuTx; kada baDi: \eng{knock at the door} kada taTuTx. 
\num{2} (moVTAru yA itara eMjinunx) (yAvudoV BAga saDilavAgi yA itara yAMtirxka doVSadiMda) dabadabisu; dabadaba baDiduko; laTalaTisu; laTalaTa sadudx mADu. 
\num{3} (yaMtarxda eMjininxna \vi) (iMdhana soPxVTada pariNAmavAgi) siDiyutitxru; BAri soPxVTagaLa sadidxna saraNiyanunx sUsu, horabiDu. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} \eng{knock about (}\engit{or} \eng{around)} 
\banum
\alnum{a} matetx matetx, meVliMda meVle, padeV padeV -- hoDe, baDi, cacucx. 
\alnum{b} (obabxnanunx) oraTAgi, niSuThxravAgi, kaThoVravAgi -- kANu; (obabxna \vi) pirxVti, dayegaLilalxde yA nidaRyavAgi vatiRsu, naDeduko: \eng{he knocked his children about} avanu tananx makakxLa bagegx nidaRyavAgi naDedukoLuLxtitxdadx. 
\alnum{c} akasAmxtAtxgi, AkasimxkavAgi--(oMdeDe) iru, hAjariru, upasithxtanAgiru. 
\alnum{d} (kelasavilalxde) aledADutitxru; sutAtxDutitxru. 
\alnum{e} avayxvasithxta bALanunx baduku; gotutx guriyilalxda jiVvana naDesu. 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{2} \eng{knock against} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (oMdakekx) baDi; Dikikx hoDe: \eng{the car knocked against a tree} kAru maravoMdakekx baDiyitu, Dikikx hoDeyitu. 
\alnum{b} (\rUpa) (obabxnanunx) akasAmxtAtxgi -- kANu, saMdhisu, eduru hAyu: \eng{I knocked against an old crony at the theatre} nATakashAleyalilx akasAmxtAtxgi nananx haLeya geLeyanobabxnanunx kaMDe. 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{3} \eng{knock back} (\birx) (\ashi) 
\banum
\alnum{a} (\kanmu\ gabagabane) tinunx; mukukx. 
\alnum{b} (\kanmu\ gaTagaTane, beVgabeVga) kuDi. 
\alnum{c} (eNike, yoVjane, kAyaRkarxma, \mo vanunx) keDisu; asatxvayxsatxgoLisu. 
\alnum{d} (AseTxrXVliya matutx nUyxsiZVleMDf) (\AmA) nirAkarisu; dhikakxrisu. 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{4} \eng{knock down} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (vayxkitx, beVTe, shaturx vimAna, \mo vanunx) hoDeduruLisu; hoDedu nelakekx biVLisu: \eng{the hunter knocked the boar down} beVDa kADuhaMdiyanunx hoDeduruLisida. \eng{knocked down by the blazing sun, he died on the spot} uribisilina hoDetadiMda avanu niMtalelxV satutx bidadx. 
\alnum{b} (kaTaTxDa \mo vanunx) keDavu; uruLisu; nelasama mADu. 
\alnum{c} (\rUpa) (vAda \mo vugaLalilx) meVlugeY sAdhisu; maNiyisu; soVlisu. 
\alnum{d} (harAjinalilx sutitxge baDidu) savAludAranige vasutxvanunx -- biDu, koDu, vahisu. 
\alnum{e} (\AmA) (obabxnanunx hADalu) kUgi -- kare, koVru. 
\alnum{f} (\AmA) (vasutxvina) (bele) iLisu; tagigxsu; kaDime mADu. 
\alnum{g} (\ame) (\ashi) kadi; lapaTAyisu; egarisu. 
\alnum{h} (vANijayx) (ravAneyalilx jAga uLisalu yaMtarx, piVThoVpakaraNa, \mo vugaLa) BAgagaLanunx -- beVpaRDisu; kaLaci hAku. 
\alnum{i} (AseTxrXVliya matutx nUyxsiZVleMDf) (\ashi) (saMbaLada cekakxnunx, haNavanunx) uDAyisu; KacuR mADi biDu. 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{5} \eng{knock off} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (tale \mo vanunx) hoDeduruLisu; ETu koTuTx keDavu; hoDedu hAku: \eng{knock person's head off} (obabxna) tale hArisu; tale kaDidu hAku. 
\alnum{b} (\rUpa) (obabxnanunx) sulaBavAgi soVlisu; sarAgavAgi miVrisu; sharxmavilalxdaMte tale meTuTx. 
\alnum{c} kelasa mugisade nililxsu, sathxgitagoLisu: \eng{we knocked off at 5.30} nAvu aidUvarege kelasa nililxsidevu, sathxgitagoLisidevu. 
\alnum{d} (kelasavanunx) (mADi) mugisu; samApitxgoLisu; konegoLisu; pUNaR mADu: \eng{knocked off work early} beVga kelasa mugisidevu. 
\alnum{e} (\AmA) (vayxvahAravanunx) beVgabeVga, avasaravasaravAgi, tavxreyiMda -- mADi mugisu, pUNaRgoLisu. 
\alnum{f} (\AmA) (padayx \mo vanunx) beVga beVga racisu; avasaravasaravAgi heNe, tayArisu. 
\alnum{g} (bele, bilulx, \mo vugaLiMda gotAtxda mobalaganunx) kaDime mADu; kaDidu hAku; vajA mADu. 
\alnum{h} (\ashi) kadi; egarisu; lapaTAyisu. 
\alnum{i} (\birx) (\ashi) (heMgasanunx) keVyu; saMBoVgisu. 
\alnum{j} (\ashi) kolulx; koMdu hAku. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{6} \eng{knock on} (ragibx ceMDATadalilx) eduru pakaSxda goVlinatatx (ceMDanunx) keYyiMdaloV, toVLiniMdaloV taLuLx, dUDu, nUku. 
\numi{7} \eng{knock out} 
\banum
\alnum{a} cuMgANiyanunx (kuTiTx yA taTiTx) -- baridu mADu, KAli mADu; (adaralilxna bUdi, karaku, \mo vanunx) koDavu. 
\alnum{b} taleya meVle moTiTx, hoDedu--(obabxnige) parxjecnx tapipxsu, (obabxnanunx) mUCeR hoVgisu. 
\alnum{c} (muSiTxkALagadalilx) (\sA\ hatetxNisuvudaroLagAgi) meVleVLadaMte (malalxnanunx)--hoDedu keDavu; hoDeduruLisu. 
\alnum{d} (\rUpa) (\kanmu\ sapxdhARtamxka paMdayxdalilx) soVlisu. 
\alnum{e} niSapxrXyoVjakagoLisu; nirupayukatxvAgisu; kelasakekx bAradaMte mADu. 
\alnum{f} (\ashi) beragugoLisu; cakitagoLisu; acacxrigoLisu; AshacxyaR huTiTxsu. 
\alnum{g} (\ashi) (\AtAmx) susAtxgu; susutx mADiko; daNidu hoVgu: \eng{knocked themselves out swimming} Iji susutx mADikoMDaru. 
\alnum{h} (\AmA) (yoVjane \mo vanunx) avasaravasaravAgi mADu; avasaradalilx -- racisu, nimiRsu, rUpisu, tayArisu. 
\alnum{i} (AseTxrXVliya matutx nUyxsiZVleMDf, \ame, \ashi)gaLisu; saMpAdisu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{8} \eng{knock sideways} (\AmA) beragugoLisu; acacxri huTiTxsu. 
\num{9} \eng{knock together} avasaravasaravAgi -- kale hAku, oTiTxge seVrisu: \eng{he knocked together 50 runs} avanu avasaravasaravAgi \eng{50} ranunxgaLanunx seVrisida. 
\num{10} \eng{knock under} maNi; sharaNAgu; soVlopipxko; adhiVnanAgu. 
\numi{11} \eng{knock up} 
\banum
\alnum{a} hoDedu meVlakekx dUDu, taLuLx, Erisu. 
\alnum{b} avasaravasaravAgi mADu yA EpaRDisu. 
\alnum{c} (kirxkeTf) beVga beVga, kiSxparxvAgi (ranunxgaLanunx)--mADu, gaLisu. 
\alnum{d} (\birx) bAgilu taTiTx, kuTiTx, baDidu (malagiruvavananunx)-- ebibxsu, ecacxragoLisu. 
\alnum{e} susAtxgu; daNidu hoVgu. 
\alnum{f} susAtxgisu; daNisu; susutx mADu. 
\alnum{g} (\ame) (\ashi) basiru mADu; basirAgisu. 
\alnum{h} (ceMDATagaLalilx) paMdayx vidhuyxkatxvAgi shuruvAguvudakikxMta muMce aBAyxsa naDesu, mADu; aBAyxsakAkxgi ceMDanunx alilxMdililxge -- hoDeyutitxru yA odeyutitxru. 
\eanum
\numie
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\nuga}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{knock into a cocked hat} (yAvudanenxV yA yAranenxV) pUtiR -- soVlisu, miVrisu, jajijx hAku. 
\numi{2} \eng{knock into} \hyperref{kandict_s.pdf}{S}{shape(2) pagu(2)}{$^2$shape}. (yAranenxV yA yAvudanenxV) 
\banum
\alnum{a} sariyAda rUpakekx taru; utatxma sithxtige taru. 
\alnum{b} dashaRniVyavAgisu; aMdavAgi kANuvaMte mADu. 
\alnum{c} dakaSxvAgiruvaMte, samathaRvAgiruvaMte -- mADu. 
\hyperdef{K}{knock(1) nuga(3)}{} 
\eanum
\numie
\num{3} \eng{knock one into the middle of next week} hoDedaTuTx; ododxVDisu. 
\numi{4} \eng{knock one's head against} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (goVDe \mo vakekx) tale -- baDiduko, tAkisiko. 
\alnum{b} (parxtikUla GaTane, parisithxtigaLoDane) hoVrADu; ahita GaSaRNege baru; tale cacicxko. 
\eanum
\numie
\numi{5} \eng{knock on the head} 
\banum
\alnum{a} taleya meVle cacicx yA baDidu (vayxkitxyanunx) mUCeR hoVgisu yA kolulx. 
\alnum{b} (\rUpa) (haMcike, yoVjane, \mo vanunx) tale etatxdaMte mADu; meTuTx; aDagisu; nAshagoLisu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{6} \eng{knock spots off} sulaBavAgi soVlisu. 
\num{7} \eng{knock the} \hyperref{kandict_b.pdf}{B}{bottom(1) nuga(7)}{$^1$bottom out of} (vAda \mo vanunx) buDavilalxdedxMdu, nirAdhAraveMdu, nirupayukatxveMdu -- toVrisu, sAdhisu, parxmANiVkarisu.

\bentry
\word[know(1)]{know}
\pron{noV}
\gl{\kirx}
{(\BU\ \eng{knew} \ucAcx\ nUyx; \BUkaq\ \eng{known} \ucAcx\ noVnf).}

\gl{\sakirx}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (yAreMbudanunx, yAvudeMbudanunx) ari; kaMDuko; tiLiduko; gurutisu: \eng{I knew him at once} avanu yAreMbudanunx takaSxNa tiLidukoMDe. \eng{I knew him for an Englishman} avanu AMgalxneMbudanunx kaMDukoMDe. \eng{will you know him again?} avananunx matotxmemx gurutisabalelxyA? 
\num{2} viveVcanAshakitx hoMdiru; (vayxkitxyanunx vayxkitxyiMda, vasutxvanunx vasutxviniMda) beVpaRDisi gurutisu; (avugaLa parasapxra) vayxtAyxsa, tAratamayx, BeVda -- tiLi, ari: \eng{know right from wrong} sarigU tapipxgU naDuvaNa (parasapxra) BeVda tiLi. 
\num{3} (vayxkitx, vasutx, sathxLagaLa) paricaya hoMdiru; (avugaLanunx) tiLidiru, tiLidavanAgiru, balalxvanAgiru: \eng{I know him by sight} Atananunx keVvala noVDidedxVne aSeTx; nanage avana muKaparicaya ide. \eng{I know him to speak to} Atananunx mAtanADisuvaSuTx balelx. 
\num{4} (Baya, noVvu, \mo vanunx savxMta anuBavadiMda) aritiru; tiLidavanAgiru; balalxvanAgiru. 
\num{5} oLapaTiTxru; oLagAgiru; \eng{her joy knew no bounds} avaLa AnaMdakekx pAraveV iralilalx. 
\num{6} AtimxVyavAgi tiLidiru; nikaTa yA AtimxVya paricaya hoMdiru: \eng{they are our neighbours, but we don't know them} avaru namamx nereyavaru, Adare namage avara nikaTa paricaya ilalx. 
\num{7} (\pArxparx) saMBoVgisu; meYthuna naDesu. 
\num{8} tiLidiru; aritiru; tiLidukoMDiru; anuBava yA Odu yA sudidxya PalavAgi (yAvudanenxV) manasisxnalilx yA nenapinalilx iTuTxkoMDiru, hoMdiru: \eng{doesn't know your address} ninanx viLAsa tiLidukoMDilalx, gotitxlalx. \eng{knows a lot about cars} kArugaLa viSaya bahaLa aritidAdxne. \eng{know what to do} Enu mADabeVkeMdu gotitxru. 
\num{9} (saMgatiyoMdara) arivu -- paDediru, hoMdiru; balalxvanAgiru; gotitxru: \eng{he konws I am waiting} nAnu kAyutitxruvudu avanige arivide; nAnu kAyutitxdedxVneMbudu avanige gotitxde. 
\num{10} (BASe, viSaya, \mo vugaLalilx) pAMDitayx hoMdiru; parxButavx paDediru; niSANxtanAgiru; oLeLxya tiLivaLike hoMdiru; seYdAdhxMtika yA pArxyoVgika jAcnxna hoMdiru. \eng{knows German} jamaRnf BASeyanunx cenAnxgi tiLidukoMDidAdxne. \eng{knows his tables} koVSaTxkagaLalilx niSANxtanAgidAdxne. 
\num{11} KacitavAgi BAvisu; KAtariyAgi eNisu: \eng{I know it must be somewhere here} adu ilelxV elolxV irabeVkeMdu nanage KacitavAgide. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\akirx}
\bmng
tiLidukoMDiru; aritiru. 
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\nuga}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} \eng{all one knows (how)} 
\banum
\alnum{a} tiLidadadxnenxlalx. 
\alnum{b} tAnu mADabahudAdadxnenxlalx; tananx shakitxpUtiR. 
\alnum{c} keYlAda maTiTxgU; tananx savaRshakitxyiMdalU AguvaSuTx maTiTxge. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} \eng{before one knows where one is} digaBxrXmegoLisuvaSuTx shiVGarxvAgi; kaMgeDisuvaSuTx kiSxparxvAgi; kakAkxbikikx mADuvaSuTx beVga. 
\numi{3} \eng{be not to know} 
\banum
\alnum{a} yAvudeV riVtiyalilx tiLiyalAgadaMtiru; tiLidukoLuLxva -- mAgaR, vidhAna, rahA ilalxdiru: \eng{wasn't to know they'd arrive late} avaru taDavAgi barutAtxreMdu tiLidukoLaLxlAgalilalx. 
\alnum{b} (obabxnige) heVLakUDadaMtiru; tiLisabAradaMtiru: \eng{she's not to know about the party} saMtoVSakUTada viSaya avaLige tiLisabAradu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{4} \eng{don't I know it?} (\AmA) (viSAdadiMda opipxkoLuLxva, samamxtisuva mAtAgi) nanage gotitxlalxveV? nanage tiLiyadeV? (gotitxde, manasisxlalxdidadxrU opipxkoLaLxbeVkAgide eMbathaRdalilx). 
\num{5} \eng{don't you know?} (mAtina naDuve seVrisuva nirathaRka padagucaCxvAgi) ninage gotitxlalxveV? ninage tiLiyadeV?: \eng{It is such a bore, don't you know?} adoMdu shudadhx beVjArina saMgati, ninage gotitxlalxveV? 
\num{6} \eng{for all (}\engit{or} \eng{aught) I know} nanage tiLidiruva maTiTxge; nananx arivige saMbaMdhisiruva maTiTxge. 
\numi{7} \hyperref{kandict_g.pdf}{G}{god(1) pagu(12)}{$^1$god} \engit{or} \hyperref{kandict_h.pdf}{H}{heaven pagu(6)}{heaven} \engit{or} \eng{the} \hyperref{kandict_l.pdf}{L}{Lord(1) pagu(14)}{$^1$lord (only) knows}

\alnum{a} (nananx yA matayxRmAnavana arivige, manuSayxna arivige miVridudx eMbudanunx sUcisalu heVLuva mAtu) deVvarobabxnige gotutx; BagavaMta mAtarx balalx.

\numie
\num{8} \eng{has been known to do} mADutAtxneMdu gotAtxgide, parxsidadhxvAgide: \eng{he has been known to be unreliable} avanu vishAvxsAhaRnalalx eMbudu gotAtxgide. 
\num{9} \eng{I knew it} nanage adu gotitxtutx. adu AgiyeV AgutatxdeMdu nanage KAtariyAgitutx, KacitavAgi tiLiditutx. 
\num{10} \eng{I know what} EneMbudu nanage gotutx; muMdiDalu yA maMDisalu nananxlilx, nananx hatitxra, nananx baLi oMdu hosa kalapxne, aBipArxya yA sUcane uMTu, ide. 
\num{11} \eng{know about} (oMdara, obabxna) viSayavanunx tiLidiru; samAcAra aritiru.

\banum

\alnum{b} curukubudidhxyavanAgiru; sUkaSxmX parijAcnxna hoMdiru.

\num{14} \eng{know best} itararigiMta hecucx tiLidavanu \mo vanu Agiru yA hAge heVLiko. 
\num{15} \eng{know better (than that)} adakikxMta hecucx gotitxru; adanunx naMbadiruvaSuTx, aMte naDedukoLaLxdiruvaSuTx tiLidukoMDiru.

\banum

\banum

\num{26} \eng{know the ropes (}\engit{or} \eng{one's stuff)} yAvudAdarU oMdu kAyaRkeSxVtarxda parisithxtiyanunx, vidayxmAnagaLanunx tiLidiru; (keYkoMDa kelasada yA viSayada) vivaragaLa yA vidayxmAnagaLa pUNaR paricaya hoMdiru; oMdu kelasa mADuva riVtiyanunx tiLidiru. 
\num{27} \eng{know what one is talking about} (\AmA) Enu mAtanADutitxdedxVye, heVLutitxdidxVye eMbudanunx tiLidiru; anuBavadiMda yA anuBavaviruva viSayavanunx mAtarx kuritu mAtanADu. 
\hyperdef{K}{know(1) nuga(28)}{} 
\num{28} \eng{know what's what} loVkAnuBava hoMdiru; vayxvahAra jAcnxnaviru; Enu, etatx enunxvudanunx tiLidiru; parxpaMcada vasutx matutx vayxvahAragaLa bagegx sariyAda yA sAkaSuTx sAmAnayx jAcnxna hoMdiru; yAvudu Enu eMbudanunx aritiru. 
\num{29} \eng{know who's who} parxtiyobabx vayxkitxyU yAru Enu eMbudanunx aritiru, tiLidiru. 
\num{30} \eng{let it be known} tiLiyuvaMtAgali; tiLiyapaDisali; parxkaTisali. 
\num{31} \eng{let me know} nanage -- tiLisu, tiLiyapaDisu, tiLiyaheVLu, tiLiyuvaMte mADu. 
\num{32} \eng{make oneself known to somebody} yAroV obabxrige tananx paricaya mADisiko. 
\num{33} \eng{not if I know it} nananx iceCxge, saMkalapxkekx virudadhxvAgi mAtarx. 
\num{34} \eng{not know any better} (sariyAda shikaSxNa, anuBava, \mo vu ilalxda kAraNa) sariyAgi, saBayxvAgi -- vatiRsadiru. 
\num{35} \eng{not know(one) from} \hyperref{kandict_a.pdf}{A}{adam(1) nuga(1)}{$^1$adam} nanage avana guruteV ilalx; avanu heVgidAdxneMbudeV nanage tiLiyadu. 
\num{36} \eng{not know that...} (\AmA) KacitavAgilalxdiru; sAkaSuTx daqDhavAgilalxdiru: \eng{I don't know that I want to go} hoVgabeVkeniside eMdu nanage KacitavAgilalx. 
\numi{37} \eng{not know that hit one} 
\banum
\alnum{a} idadxkikxdadxMte hatanAgu; haThAtAtxgi kolalxlapxDu; idadxkikxdadxMte koleyAgu. 
\alnum{b} pUtiR digaBxrXmegoLuLx; kakAkxbikikxyAgu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{38} \eng{not want to know} (oMdakekx) gamana -- koDadiru, harisadiru; tiLiyalu iciCxsadiru; ariyalu iSaTxpaDadiru. 
\num{39} \eng{that's all you know (about that)} ninage (adara bagegx) gotitxruvudelalx aSeTxV; niVnu aMdukoMDiruvudakikxMtalU hecucx daDaDx, BAvisikoMDiruvudakikxMtalU hecucx ajacnx. 
\num{40} \eng{ what do you know (about that)?} (\AmA\ AshacxyaRsUcakavAgi) ninage (adara bagegx) Enu gotutx, Enu tiLidide? 
\num{41} \eng{you know} (\AmA) (keVLuganige A viSaya gotutx yA avanu adanunx tiLidukoLaLxbeVkAgitutx eMbudanunx nenapu mADalu yA saMBASaNeya naDuvaNa terapanunx tuMbuva mAtAgi baLasuva) ninage, ninageV yA ninagU -- gotutx, tiLidide. 
\num{42} \eng{you know something (}\engit{or} \eng{what)?} nAnu ninage oMdu viSaya heVLalidedxVne. 
\num{43} \eng{you know what he} \engit{or} \eng{it is} avanu yA adu Enu enunxvudu ninage gotutx; ninage avana yA adara guNAvaguNagaLu, jaTila savxBAva, savxrUpa, \mo vu gotutx, avugaLa paricayavide. 
\num{44} \hyperref{kandict_y.pdf}{Y}{you pagu(3)}{you know-what (or-who)} (yArU, yAvudu eMdu niSakxqqSaTxvAgi heVLade adhAyxhAravAgiruvalilx) `ninage gotatxlalx, yArU (yA yAvudu) aMta?' 
\num{45} \eng{you never know} muMdeVnu enunxvudu KacitavAgi gotAtxgadu; BaviSayx anishicxta; nALeyadu pUtiR KAtariyAgi tiLiyuvudilalx. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry
